०५ तत्त्वत्रयचिन्तनाधिकारः
॥ श्रीः ॥
॥ श्रीमते निगमान्तमहादेशिकाय नमः ॥

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

॥ श्रीमद्रहस्यत्रयसारे तत्त्वत्रयचिन्तनाधिकारः ॥ ५ ॥

विश्वास-टिप्पनी

चिन्तन-शब्द-प्रयोगेण पूर्वपक्षोल्लेखादि-सहितो विस्तार उच्यते।

मूलम्

॥ श्रीमद्रहस्यत्रयसारे तत्त्वत्रयचिन्तनाधिकारः ॥ ५ ॥

English

(5) THE CHAPTER ON THE THREE ‘REALS’ (OR TATVAS) page107

प्रयोजनम्

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः (सं॰प॰)

+++(चिद्-अचिद्-ईश्वरेषु भ्रान्ति-द्वयम् …)+++
प्रकृत्य्-आत्म-भ्रान्तिर् गलति चिद्-अचिल्-लक्षण-धिया,
तथा जीवेशैक्य-प्रभृति-कलहस् तद्+++(=जीवेश)+++-विभजनात् +++(गलति)+++ ।
+++(“भोक्ता भोग्यं प्रेरितारञ्च मत्वा सर्वं प्रोक्तं त्रिविधं ब्रह्ममेतत् ।“→)+++
अतो +++(जीवः→)+++ भोक्ता, भोग्यं, तद्-उभय-नियन्तेति निगमैर्
विभक्तं नस् तत्त्व-त्रयम् उपदिशन्त्य् अक्षत-धियः ॥ १४ ॥

English

The delusion that the soul is nothing but the body and the senses (prakṛti)
disappears when one has a knowledge of the distinctive features of sentient beings and non-sentient things.
So also the disputes on such questions as the unity of the jīva and God will no longer continue,
when the characteristic features of each of them are marked out.
Our ācārya-s, whose wisdom never failed,
teach us about the existence of three realities (Tattvas)
classified in the s’āstrās as the experiencing subjects (bhoktā), the objects of experience and enjoyment (bhogyam)
and He who rules over both of them (Iśvara).

Español

The delusion that the soul is nothing but the body and the senses (prakṛti)
disappears when one has a knowledge of the distinctive features of sentient beings and non-sentient things.
So also the disputes on such questions as the unity of the jīva and God will no longer continue,
when the characteristic features of each of them are marked out.
Our ācārya-s, whose wisdom never failed,
teach us about the existence of three realities (Tattvas)
classified in the s’āstrās as the experiencing subjects (bhoktā), the objects of experience and enjoyment (bhogyam)
and He who rules over both of them (Iśvara).

मूलम् (सं॰प॰)

प्रकृत्यात्मभ्रान्तिर्गलति चिदचिल्लक्षणधिया
तथा जीवेशैक्यप्रभृतिकलहस्तद्विभजनात् ।
अतो भोक्ता भोग्यं तदुभयनियन्तेति निगमै
र्विभक्तं नस्तत्वत्रयमुपदिशन्त्यक्षतधियः ॥ १४ ॥

English

CLASSIFICATION OF TATVAS OR REALS AND ITS USE:

Español

CLASSIFICATION OF TATVAS OR REALS AND ITS USE:

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

+++(शरीर-शरीरि-)+++संबन्धमुम्, +++(प्राप्य-प्राप्तृ-फलोपाय-विघ्नाः→)+++ अर्थ-पञ्चकम् उङ् +गूड,
आऱु अर्थम् अऱिय-वेण्डिय् इरुक्क
इवट्रिल् एकदेशम् आन +++(चिद्-अचिद्-ईश्वर←)+++तत्व-त्रयत्तै
मुमुक्षुवुक्कु विशेषित्त् अऱिय वेणुम् ऎण्ड्रु
आचार्यर्गळ् उपदेशित्तुप् पोरुगैक्
कडिय्+++(=बीजम्)+++ ऎन्न् ऎन्निल्;

अदुक्क् अडि प्रकृत्य्-आत्म-भ्रमम् उम्
स्वतन्त्रात्म-भ्रमम् उम्
इदुक्कु निदानम् आन अनीश्वर-वाद-रुचिय् उम्
आगिऱ महा-विरोधिगळै
मुऱ्+++(←न्)+++-‌पडक्क्+++(=स्पर्शम्)+++ अऴिक्क प्राप्तम् आगै.+++(4)+++

English

It may be asked -

why the ācāryas should state that the three tatvās or ‘reals’ should be specially prescribed for the study of those who seek mokṣa , when they form only a part of the six things that should be known, namely, the five truths arthapañcaka and the relationship of soul and body (which exists between God and the world)?

The answer is as follows:

It is necessary to root out the delusion that the body is the atma and that the jīva is independent (of the Lord), as well as the view that there is no God, which is the cause of that delusion, for these are great obstacles to mokṣa.

मूलम्

संबन्धमुम् अर्थपञ्चकमुङ्गूड आऱु अर्थमऱियवेण्डियिरुक्क इवट्रिल् एकदेशमान तत्वत्रयत्तै मुमुक्षुवुक्कु विशेषित्तऱिय वेणुम् ऎण्ड्रु आचार्यर्गळुपदेशित्तुप्पोरुगैक् कडियॆन्नॆन्निल्; अदुक्कडि प्रकृत्यात्मभ्रममुम् स्वतन्त्रात्मभ्रममुम् इदुक्कु निदानमान अनीश्वरवादरुचियुमागिऱ महाविरोधिगळै मुऱ्‌पडक्कऴिक्क प्राप्तमागै.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

इत्तै निनैत्तु
भोक्तृ-भोग्य-नियन्तृ-रूपत्ताल् ए
शास्त्रङ्गळिले तत्व-विवेकम् पण्णुगिऱदु.

English

The śāstrās, therefore, divide Reality into three classes ; the experiencing subject, the object of experience or enjoyment, and the Ruler who controls and directs them.

Español

The śāstrās, therefore, divide Reality into three classes ; the experiencing subject, the object of experience or enjoyment, and the Ruler who controls and directs them.

मूलम्

इत्तै निनैत्तु भोक्तृभोग्य-नियन्तृरूपत्ताले शास्त्रङ्गळिले तत्वविवेकम् पण्णुगिऱदु.

अचित्

English

Among them, non-sentient things which are the objects of experience are of three kinds (1) Prakṛti or matter which has the three qualities of sattvam, rajas and tamas (2) Kala or time and (3) Śuddha Satvam, the substance of which the transcendental region beyond matter called Vaikuṇṭha is made.

Español

Among them, non-sentient things which are the objects of experience are of three kinds (1) Prakṛti or matter which has the three qualities of sattvam, rajas and tamas (2) Kala or time and (3) Śuddha Satvam, the substance of which the transcendental region beyond matter called Vaikuṇṭha is made.

प्रकृतिः

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

इवट्रिल् वैत्तुक्कॊण्डु

“अचेतना परार्था च
नित्या सतत-विक्रिया ।
त्रि-गुणा कर्मिणां क्षेत्रं
प्रकृते रूपम् उच्यते ॥” (परमसंहिता.)

English

The nature of (1) Prakṛti has been thus described :-

“It is 1 non-sentient (achetana).
It exists (always) for others and it is eternal,
but subject always to change or modification.
It has three qualities sattvam, rajas and tamas
and is the field of action (karma) for the jīva”.

मूलम्

इवट्रिल् वैत्तुक्कॊण्डु “अचेतना परार्था च नित्या सततविक्रिया । त्रिगुणा कर्मिणां क्षेत्रं प्रकृते रूपमुच्यते ॥” (परमसंहिता.)

कालः

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

“अनादिर् भगवान् कालो
नान्तोऽस्य द्विज विद्यते”
(वि-पु. 1-2-26),

English

The nature of (2) Kala or time is described thus :- " Bhagavān 2 Kala (i.e.) Time, which is the body of Bhagavān, has no beginning nor end.”

Español

The nature of (2) Kala or time is described thus :- " Bhagavān 2 Kala (i.e.) Time, which is the body of Bhagavān, has no beginning nor end.”

मूलम्

“अनादिर्भगवान् कालो नान्तोऽस्य द्विज विद्यते” (वि-पु. 1-2-26),

शुद्ध-सत्त्वम्

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

“कला-मुहूर्तादिमयश् च कालो
न यद्-+++(नित्य-)+++विभूतेः परिणाम-हेतुः”
(वि-पु. 4-1-84),

English

“It takes 3 the forms of such divisions as kalaa and muhoortha which are respectively 1-3/8 minutes and 1/30th part of a day (and is the cause of the modifications of matter). But it causes no change or modification in the transcendental world (Aprākritaloka) beyond matter”.

Español

“It takes 3 the forms of such divisions as kalaa and muhoortha which are respectively 1-3/8 minutes and 1/30th part of a day (and is the cause of the modifications of matter). But it causes no change or modification in the transcendental world (Aprākritaloka) beyond matter”.

मूलम्

“कलामुहूर्तादिमयश्च कालो न यद्विभूतेः परिणामहेतुः” (वि-पु. 4-1-84),

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

+++(स्वयम्प्रकाशत्वम्←)+++“ज्ञानानन्दमया लोकाः” (पाञ्चरात्रम्),

English

The nature of the transcendental world beyond matter is such that it is made of s’uddha sattvam. The world 4 made of it is of the nature of jñāna and bliss.

Español

The nature of the transcendental world beyond matter is such that it is made of s’uddha sattvam. The world 4 made of it is of the nature of jñāna and bliss.

मूलम्

“ज्ञानानन्दमया लोकाः” (पाञ्चरात्रम्),

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

“कालं स पचते तत्र +++(द्रव्य-परिणामादिषु)+++
न कालस् तत्र वै प्रभुः +++(अपि तु भगवत्-सङ्कल्पः)+++” (भार-शान्ति. 196-9.)

English

God controls time there ; time is not the 5 cause of any change or modification in the world of Śuddha-sattvam (as it is in the world of matter).

Español

God controls time there ; time is not the 5 cause of any change or modification in the world of Śuddha-sattvam (as it is in the world of matter).

मूलम्

“कालं स पचते तत्र न कालस्तत्र वै प्रभुः” (भार-शान्ति. 196-9.)

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

इत्यादिगळिल् ए
त्रि-गुण–काल–शुद्ध-सत्त्व-रूपङ्गळ् आन त्रि-विधाचेतनङ्गळ्-उडैय स्वभावञ् चॊल्लिट्रु.

English

Thus the nature of Prakṛti, Kāla and Śuddha sattva which belong to three classes of non-sentient things (achetana), has been described.

Español

Thus the nature of Prakṛti, Kāla and Śuddha sattva which belong to three classes of non-sentient things (achetana), has been described.

मूलम्

इत्यादिगळिले त्रिगुणकालशुद्धसत्त्वरूपङ्गळान त्रिविधाचेतनङ्गळुडैय स्वभावञ् चॊल्लिट्रु.

जीवः

English

NOW FOR THE EXPERIENCING SUBJECT OR JĪVA:

Español

NOW FOR THE EXPERIENCING SUBJECT OR JĪVA:

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

“पुमान् न देवो न नरः” (वि-पु. 2-13-98.),

English

“The jivātma is 6 neither a god nor a man”;

Español

“The jivātma is 6 neither a god nor a man”;

मूलम्

“पुमान्न देवो न नरः” (वि-पु. 2-13-98.),

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

“नायं देवो न मर्त्यो वा”(),

English

“He is 7 neither a god nor a man”.
(That is: These distinctions are based only on the respective bodies, whereas the soul within has no such distinctions.)

Español

“He is 7 neither a god nor a man”.
(That is: These distinctions are based only on the respective bodies, whereas the soul within has no such distinctions.)

मूलम्

“नायं देवो न मर्त्यो वा”(),

बद्धः, मुक्तः

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

“क्षरस् सर्वाणि भूतानि
कुटस्थोऽक्षर उच्यते” (गीता 15-16)

English

The jīva is of three kinds :-

Baddha or the soul in bondage is called in the Gita “Kshara”
(because he is in contact with matter which is subject to change)
All beings8 (from Brahma to the blade of grass) are ‘Ksharas’ or Baddhas.

The mukta or the soul which has obtained release from contact with matter
is no longer subject to change and is called akṣara or Kootastha (because it is imputable).

Español

The jīva is of three kinds :-

Baddha or the soul in bondage is called in the Gita “Kshara”
(because he is in contact with matter which is subject to change)
All beings8 (from Brahma to the blade of grass) are ‘Ksharas’ or Baddhas.

The mukta or the soul which has obtained release from contact with matter
is no longer subject to change and is called akṣara or Kootastha (because it is imputable).

मूलम्

“क्षरस्सर्वाणि भूतानि कुटस्थोऽक्षर उच्यते” (गीता 15-16)

नित्य-सूरिः

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

“यद्वै पश्यन्ति सूरयः” (वि-पु. 1-6-39)

English

The third class of jīvas are the Sūris9 who are described as seeing eternally the transcendental world beyond matter.

Español

The third class of jīvas are the Sūris9 who are described as seeing eternally the transcendental world beyond matter.

मूलम्

“यद्वै पश्यन्ति सूरयः” (वि-पु. 1-6-39)

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

इत्य्-आदिगळाले त्रिविध-जीवर्गळ्-उडैय प्रकारम् विवेकिक्कप्-पट्टदु.

मूलम्

इत्यादिगळाले त्रिविधजीवर्गळुडैय प्रकारम् विवेकिक्कप्पट्टदु.

ईश्वरः

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

“सर्वज्ञस् सर्व-दृक् सर्व-
शक्ति-ज्ञान-बलर्द्धिमान् ।
क्लम-तन्द्रा-भय-क्रोध-
कामादिभिर् असंयुतः ॥”
(वि-पु. 5-1-46)

इत्य्-आदिगळाल् ए ईश्वर-स्वभावम् उपदिष्टम् आयिट्रु.

English

The third class of ‘Real’ is Iśvara who has been thus described :-
He is all ;10
He knows all;
He sees all;
He possesses all strength, all knowledge, all power, all wealth :
He is without fatigue, without lassitude,
without fear, without anger, without desire and other such (blemishes).
Thus has the nature of Iśvara been taught,

Español

The third class of ‘Real’ is Iśvara who has been thus described :-
He is all ;10
He knows all;
He sees all;
He possesses all strength, all knowledge, all power, all wealth :
He is without fatigue, without lassitude,
without fear, without anger, without desire and other such (blemishes).
Thus has the nature of Iśvara been taught,

मूलम्

“सर्वज्ञस्सर्वदृक्सर्वशक्ति-ज्ञानबलर्द्धिमान् । क्लमतन्द्री भयक्रोधकामादिभिरसंयुतः ॥” (वि-पु. 5-1-46) इत्यादिगळाले ईश्वरस्वभावम् उपदिष्टमायिट्रु.

स्वाधीन-त्रि-विध-चेतनाचेतन–स्व-रूप–स्थिति-प्रवृत्ति-भेदः

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

इव्व्-ईशेशितव्य-रूपम् आन तत्त्व-त्रयम् निऱ्‌कुम् निलैयै

“स्वाधीन–त्रि-विध+++(←चेतने, अचेतने च)+++–चेतनाचेतन–स्व-रूप–स्थिति-प्रवृत्ति-भेदम् +++(विष्णुम् …)+++”

ऎण्ड्रु सुरुङ्ग+++(=शृङ्गम्)+++ अरुळिच् चॆय्दार्.

English

Thus the three realities consist of the Ruler and the Ruled (the latter including prakṛti and the sentient beings) and our ācārya s (Śrī Yāmunācārya and Śrī Rāmānujācārya) have stated this concisely in the words

“(Iśvara)11 on whom depend the essential nature (svarūpa), the continuance (sthiti) and the activity (pravṛtti) of the three kinds of sentient beings and of non-sentient things with all their differences”.

Español

Thus the three realities consist of the Ruler and the Ruled (the latter including prakṛti and the sentient beings) and our ācārya s (Śrī Yāmunācārya and Śrī Rāmānujācārya) have stated this concisely in the words

“(Iśvara)11 on whom depend the essential nature (svarūpa), the continuance (sthiti) and the activity (pravṛtti) of the three kinds of sentient beings and of non-sentient things with all their differences”.

मूलम्

इव्वीशेशितव्यरूपमान तत्त्वत्रयम् निऱ्‌कुम् निलैयै “स्वाधीनत्रिविधचेतनाचेतनस्वरूपस्थितिप्रवृत्तिभेदम्” ऎण्ड्रु सुरुङ्ग अरुळिच्चॆय्दार्.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

त्रि-विध-चेतनर् ऎण्ड्रदु
बद्धरैय् उम् मुक्तरैय् उम् नित्यरैय् उम्.

English

The three kinds of sentient beings are those that are in bondage (baddha), those that have obtained release (mukta) and those that are eternally free (nitya).

Español

The three kinds of sentient beings are those that are in bondage (baddha), those that have obtained release (mukta) and those that are eternally free (nitya).

मूलम्

त्रिविधचेतनरॆण्ड्रदु बद्धरैयुम् मुक्तरैयुम् नित्यरैयुम्.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

त्रि-विधाचेतनम् ऎण्ड्रदु
त्रि-गुण-द्रव्यत्तैय् उम्, कालत्तैय् उम्, शुद्ध-सत्त्वम् आन द्रव्यत्तैय् उम्.

English

The three kinds of non-sentient things are Prakṛti with its three qualities (sattvam, rajas and tamas), Time, and Śuddhasattvam.

Español

The three kinds of non-sentient things are Prakṛti with its three qualities (sattvam, rajas and tamas), Time, and Śuddhasattvam.

मूलम्

त्रिविधाचेतनमॆण्ड्रदु त्रिगुणद्रव्यत्तैयुम् कालत्तैयुम् शुद्धसत्त्वमान द्रव्यत्तैयुम्.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

स्वरूपम् ऎण्ड्रदु स्वासाधारण-धर्मत्ताल् ए निरूपितम् आन धर्मियै.

English

The essential nature (svarūpa) means the substance or thing which is defined by attributes peculiar and unique to it.

Español

The essential nature (svarūpa) means the substance or thing which is defined by attributes peculiar and unique to it.

स्वरूपमॆण्ड्रदु स्वासाधारणधर्मत्ताले निरूपितमान धर्मियै.

Continuance (sthiti, means continuance of the thing or object in time.

Español

Continuance (sthiti, means continuance of the thing or object in time.

इदु-दान् +++(→स्थितिः)+++ नित्यवस्तुक्कळुक्कु नित्यैय् आय् इरुक्कुम्.

English

Activity or pravṛtti includes action and abstention from action.

Activity or pravṛtti includes action and abstention from action.

प्रमाणानि, प्रतीतिः

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

इवैय् ऎल्लाम् +++(→स्वरूप-स्थिति-प्रवृत्तयः)+++ वस्तुक्कळ्-तोऱुम्+++(=प्रत्येकतया)+++ प्रमाण-प्रतिनियतम् आय् +++(भेदेन)+++ इरुक्कुम्.

English

All these three : the essential nature (svarūpa), the continuance in time (sthithi) and the activity (pravṛtti) are seen (by perception and other pramaṇas) to be different in the case of each thing or object.

Español

मूलम्

इवैयॆल्लाम् वस्तुक्कळ् तोऱुम् प्रमाणप्रतिनियतमायिरुक्कुम्.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

इप् प्रमाणङ्गळ् वस्तुक्कळैक् काट्टुम् पोदु
अव्वो वस्तुक्कळिन् स्व-रूपत्तैय् उम्,
स्व-रूप-निरूपक-धर्मङ्गळैय् उम्,
निरूपित–स्व-रूप–विशेषणङ्गळैय् उम्,
व्यापारङ्गळैय् उङ् काट्टुम्.

English

When the pramāṇas or sources of knowledge (like perception and inference)
reveal an object or thing,
they disclose the essential Nature or svarūpa of the object,
the attributes that define it,
the (other) qualities of the object so defined
and also its activities.

Español

When the pramāṇas or sources of knowledge (like perception and inference)
reveal an object or thing,
they disclose the essential Nature or svarūpa of the object,
the attributes that define it,
the (other) qualities of the object so defined
and also its activities.

English

The essential nature is always revealed

Español

The essential nature is always revealed as endowed with the attributes that define it.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

अन्द स्व-रूपत्तैच् चॊल्लुम् पोदु अव्व्-ओ धर्मङ्गळैय् इट्ट्-अल्लदु सॊल्ल-वॊण्णादु.

English

It is not possible to speak of the essential nature of a thing (svarūpa) except in terms of the respective attributes.

Español

It is not possible to speak of the essential nature of a thing (svarūpa) except in terms of the respective attributes.

मूलम्

शश-विषाण तुल्यम् आम्.

English

To speak of an object minus its attributes would be as meaningless as to speak of a hare’s horns.

Español

To speak of an object minus its attributes would be as meaningless as to speak of a hare’s horns.

जीव-स्वरूपम्

English

THE NATURE OF THE JĪVA.

Español

THE NATURE OF THE JĪVA.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

आगैयाल् जीव-स्वरूपत्तैच्
ज्ञानत्वम् आनन्दत्वम् अमलत्वम् अणुत्वम्
इत्य्-आदिगळ् आन निरूपक-धर्मङ्गळैय् इट्टु निरूपित्तु
ज्ञानम् आनन्दम् अमलम् अणु ऎण्ड्रु
इम्-मुखङ्गळाल् ए सॊल्लक् कडवदु+++(=अर्हति)+++.

English

Therefore the essential nature (svarūpa) of the jīva may be described as jñāna (knowledge), bliss (ānanda), (amala) being pure, and being atomic (aṇu) in terms of its defining attributes (i. e.) being of the nature of knowledge, being of the nature of bliss, being pure and being atomic.

Español

Therefore the essential nature (svarūpa) of the jīva may be described as jñāna (knowledge), bliss (ānanda), (amala) being pure, and being atomic (aṇu) in terms of its defining attributes (i. e.) being of the nature of knowledge, being of the nature of bliss, being pure and being atomic.

इज् जीव-तत्त्वम्

अवनुक्क् ए निरूपाधिक-शेषम् ऎण्ड्रुम्,

English

This reality, viz. the jīva is always śeṣa to Iśvara (i.e.) it exists only for Iśvara

Español

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

अयोग+++(←"अ/आय”)++++अन्य+++(←"उ”)+++-योग-व्यवच्छेदङ्गळाल् ए

संबन्धि-स्वरूपम् निरूपितम् आनाल् अल्लद् अऱिय वॊण्णामैयाल्+++(=अशक्यतया)+++ ए
जीवनुक्कु इदु निरूपित–स्व-रूप–विशेषणम् ऎन्नल् आम्.

English

Thus its existing (always) for the Lord is affirmed (ayogavyavaccheda)
and also its existing for no other than the Lord (anya yogavyavaccheda).
This quality of being śeṣa to the Lord,
which is disclosed in the first word of Tirumantra, namely om (aum),
is of the nature of a relationship ( sambandha)
and requires, therefore, a thing having that relationship
and cannot be understood without it.
So this śeṣatva may be called an additional quality of a thing,
namely, the jīva, which has already been defined by its defining attributes.

Español

and requires, therefore, a thing having that relationship

Here the definition of the jīva is that it is a thing which is sentient while being also atomic.

Español

ईश्वर-स्वरूपम्

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

English

Similarly Iśvara may be defined as having sentience along with omnipresence (vibhu).

Español

He may also be defined as one that is absolutely independent of everything else, while being the unconditional seshin (i.e.) one for whom all other things exist (unconditionally).

मूलम्

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

जीवेश्वर-रूपम् आन आत्म-वर्गत्तुक्क् ऎल्लाम्
पॊदुव्+++(=साधारणम्)+++ आन लक्षणम्

English

Español

The class of atmas which includes jīvas and Iśvara
may be defined as those that are sentient and pratyak

मूलम्

English

To be sentient is to be the possessor of knowledge.

Español

To be sentient is to be the possessor of knowledge.

मूलम्

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

English

To be subjective or inward (or pratyak) is to possess luminosity to oneself.

Español

To be subjective or inward (or pratyak) is to possess luminosity to oneself.

मूलम्

प्रत्यक्त्वमावदु तनक्कुत्तान् तोट्रुगै.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

अप्-पोदु धर्म-भूत-ज्ञान-निरपेक्षम् आग नान् ऎण्ड्रु तोट्रुम्.

English

The atmā or soul is self-luminous
and shines as ‘I’
without the help of the attributive knowledge 12 (dharmabhūta jñāna) .

The soul is of the nature of jñāna or knowledge (i.c.) its svarūpa is knowledge.
At the same time the soul has knowledge as an attribute
and this jñāna or knowledge is called Dharma bhuta jñāna or attributive knowledge.*

Español

The atmā or soul is self-luminous
and shines as ‘I’
without the help of the attributive knowledge 12 (dharmabhūta jñāna) .

The soul is of the nature of jñāna or knowledge (i.c.) its svarūpa is knowledge.
At the same time the soul has knowledge as an attribute
and this jñāna or knowledge is called Dharma bhuta jñāna or attributive knowledge.*

मूलम्

अप्पोदु धर्मभूतज्ञाननिरपेक्षमाग नानॆण्ड्रु तोट्रुम्.

विश्वास-प्रस्तुतिः

इप्-पडि चेतनत्वादिगळ्
ईश्वरनुक्क् उम्, जीवनुक्क् उम् पॊदुव्+++(=साधारणम्)+++ आगैयाल् एय्
अवनिऱ्‌-काट्टिल् व्यावृत्ति तोट्रुगैक्क् आग
जीव-लक्षणत्तिल् स्वतश्-शेषत्वादिगळ् सॊल्लुगिऱदु.

English

Since sentience and inwardness (pratyaktva)

Español
